 lekin kai raajnneetik partiyon ke virodh ke kaaran is faisle ko thande baste main daal diya gaya

 Ayodhya Case: ayodhya bhoomi vivaad ko lekar paanch jajon kii peeth ne shanivaar ko aitihaasik faisla sunaaya diya he
 The Supreme Court said that the Sunni Waqf Board was unable to prove its exclusive right to the disputed structure
 court ne vivaadit dhaanche kii jameen hindu paksh ko dene kaa faisla sunaaya he
 At the same time, he has asked the government to give five acres of land to Muslims elsewhere in Ayodhya itself
 supreme court ke yah faisla beete kai dashakon se do sumadaay ke bich maujuud gatirodh ko kam karne ke liye bade kadam kii tarah sabit ho saktaa he
 At the same time, the constitutional bench of five judges said that this court is working to resolve a dispute whose origins are as old as the idea of india
 vivaadit sthal par faisle sunaate hue peeth ne un binduon kii ore bhi ishaara kiya he jinke aadhaar par usne yah faisla diya he
 Let's take a look at the points that became the basis of this decision of the Supreme Court - the court while giving the verdict said that the basis of the situation
 hinduon kii tulana main muslim paksh vivaadit dhaanche par apana exclusive rhite ko behatar tareeke se sabit nahin kar paaya he
 “muslims were evicted from the mosque on 22 / 23 December 1949, which was finally demolished on 6 December 1992
 iske baavjood musalamaanon ne masjid ko choda nahin tha
 The court will not ignore the Muslims, who are kept as the underprivileged
 yah kanoon ke shashan ke liye patibaddh ek dharmanirpeksh raashtra main sahi nahin he
 In this regard, the Supreme said that the division of disputed land was legally untenable
 saath hi isse saamaajik shanti ko banaae rakhana bhi sambhav nahin he
 Its solution is not possible like the Allahabad High Court
 bhoomi ke vibhaajan se donon pakshon ke hiton kasngrakshan nahin hoga or shanti kii sthaayee bhaavana bhi surakshit nahin rahegi
 Destruction of public places of worship was completely wrong
 musalamaanon ko galat tareeke se ek masjid se vanchit kiya gaya, jo 450 saal pehle acchhee tarah se banaai gai thi

 The official report of the financial condition of the country in the Parliament before the budget is called Economic Survey
 aaj se shuru ho rahe bajet satr kii shuruyaat main raashtrapati pranab mukherjee subah 11 baje sansad ke donon sadanon ko sanyukt rup se sambodhit karenge
 The economic survey will be presented by the government after the President's address
 iske tahat desh kii aarthik haalat kaa puraa byora pesh kiya jaataa he
 In this survey, information is provided on all aspects such as what was the trend of development in the country, how much investment was made in which area, how much development was done in which area, how the schemes were implemented
 arthvyavastha, purvanumaan or nitigat str par chunautiyon sambandhi vistrut soochnaaon kaa bhi isamen samavesh hota he
 In it, the outline of sector-wise conditions and measures for improvement are explained
 motamoti taur par, yah surveykshan bhavishya main banaai jane vaali nitiyon ke liye ek drushtikon kaa kaam karata he

 2012 main bijepi ko 142 ward main hi jeet mili thi

 army brigadier general bryan ji watasan kii report main paaya gaya ki america sainikon ne muslimon ke pavitra granth or anya dharmik samagriyon ke saath chhedchhad kii
 The comments report main rekhaankit kiya gaya ki ‘tragedeepurn ghatana’ ‘adhikariyon or commandon’ ke bich samvaad kii kami ke kaaran hui haalanki jaanch main is baat ko ‘khaarij’ kiya gaya ki ghatana ko quran kaa apmaan karne kii vidweshpurn manshaa ke saath anjaam diya gaya
 It accused junior and middle-level officials of choosing the 'easy path' rather than choosing the 'right path'
